By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre "Pasquino" derivó de un cercano tailor que fue conocido por su sabio y intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a través de la estatua, en "el honor y la eterna memoria del pobre tailor ".

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre "Pasquino" derivó de un cercano tailor que fue conocido por su sabio y intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a través de la estatua, en "el honor y la eterna memoria del pobre tailor ".

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó que el nombre " Pasquino " derivó de un talón cercano que fue conocido por su sabio y intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a través de la estatua, en "el honor y la eterna memoria del talón pobre ".

By the mid - sixteenth century it was reported that the name " Pasquino " derived from a nearby tailor who was renowned for his wit and intellect ; speculation had it that his legacy was carried on through the statue , in " the honor and everlasting remembrance of the poor tailor " . ||| A mediados del siglo XVI se informó de que el nombre "Pasquino" derivó de un cercano tailor que fue conocido por su sabio y intelecto; la especulación tenía que su legado se llevó a través de la estatua, en "el honor y la eterna memoria del pobre tailor ".
